name:Râ€yâ€aâ€nâ€Mâ€aâ€mâ€a
info:Deluxe Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in August 2023
info:Family
info:20 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted August 30, 2023
msg:I just finished cycling around Qinghai Lake and wanted to have a good rest in the bathtub, so I booked Qinghai Yinlong Hotel. The hotel is located in the city center. When you go out, turn right and you will find Xiguan Street, where you can buy all kinds of food. It is a 10-minute walk to Wangfujing, where there are many snack stalls and souvenir shops. The hotel has a swimming pool, fitness room and billiards room, which are fully equipped. The room is large and comfortable, with a separate cloakroom. The bathroom has a bathtub, a separate shower room and a separate toilet room. The toilet is very smart. It will automatically open the toilet lid, flush and automatically latch the lid, and also has a PP washing function. The bathtub has a small TV, so you can watch dramas while taking a bath. Fruit, tea bags and toiletries are provided in the room when you check in. They are all of high quality and the room lights can be adjusted to soft or bright mode. The only drawback of the room is that the air conditioner is not cold enough, the quilt is very hot, and the pillow is too soft, so I don't sleep well. It would be better if there were different pillow options. The breakfast is excellent, with a wide variety of styles and delicious food. The ramen and dumplings are made on demand. The chef is very skillful in ramen, but the tableware only provides taiko and spoons. It would be better if knives and forks can be provided.

I booked it on the official website, but I was not allowed to comment. Since then, I have blocked Atour S.

I chose Yinlong as the end point this time, which received unanimous praise from my family. In a word, except for the price, the hardware and software of Yinlong are all five-star.

You can get drinking water at the elevator entrance by yourself, and there is also water in the room, and there are fruits in the evening. The breakfast is rich, and it is said to be until ten o'clock, but there is no sign of collecting the food at ten o'clock.

You can order food in the room, and it is very rich and tastes very good. The fries are much better than McDonald's. It should be added with seasoning.

There is a large square across the road downstairs, which is quite lively, and you can also walk along the river. The children don't want to go back.

Just like it says on the room card: Falling in love with Qinghai starts from Yinlong.
